[Psalm 1:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/1?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) BLESSED is the man that walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly, nor standeth in the way of sinners, nor sitteth in the seat of the scornful. ^c1v1

[Psalm 1:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/1?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) But his delight is in the law of the LORD; and in his law doth he meditate day and night. ^c1v2

[Psalm 1:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/1?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, that bringeth forth his fruit in his season; his leaf also shall not wither; and whatsoever he doeth shall prosper. ^c1v3

[Psalm 1:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/1?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) The ungodly are not so: but are like the chaff which the wind driveth away. ^c1v4

[Psalm 1:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/1?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Therefore the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous. ^c1v5

[Psalm 1:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/1?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) For the LORD knoweth the way of the righteous: but the way of the ungodly shall perish. ^c1v6

[Psalm 2:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) WHY do the heathen rage, and the people imagine a vain thing? ^c2v1

[Psalm 2:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) The kings of the earth set themselves, and the rulers take counsel together, against the LORD, and against his anointed, saying, ^c2v2

[Psalm 2:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Let us break their bands asunder, and cast away their cords from us. ^c2v3

[Psalm 2:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) He that sitteth in the heavens shall laugh: the Lord shall have them in derision. ^c2v4

[Psalm 2:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Then shall he speak unto them in his wrath, and vex them in his sore displeasure. ^c2v5

[Psalm 2:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Yet have I set my king upon my holy hill of Zion. ^c2v6

[Psalm 2:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) I will declare the decree: the LORD hath said unto me, Thou art my Son; this day have I begotten thee. ^c2v7

[Psalm 2:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Ask of me, and I shall give thee the heathen for thine inheritance, and the uttermost parts of the earth for thy possession. ^c2v8

[Psalm 2:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) Thou shalt break them with a rod of iron; thou shalt dash them in pieces like a potter's vessel. ^c2v9

[Psalm 2:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) Be wise now therefore, O ye kings: be instructed, ye judges of the earth. ^c2v10

[Psalm 2:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Serve the LORD with fear, and rejoice with trembling. ^c2v11

[Psalm 2:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/2?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, and ye perish from the way, when his wrath is kindled but a little.  Blessed are all they that put their trust in him. ^c2v12

[Psalm 3:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) LORD, how are they increased that trouble me!  many are they that rise up against me. ^c3v1

[Psalm 3:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Many there be which say of my soul, There is no help for him in God.  Selah. ^c3v2

[Psalm 3:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) But thou, O LORD, art a shield for me; my glory, and the lifter up of mine head. ^c3v3

[Psalm 3:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) I cried unto the LORD with my voice, and he heard me out of his holy hill.  Selah. ^c3v4

[Psalm 3:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) I laid me down and slept; I awaked; for the LORD sustained me. ^c3v5

[Psalm 3:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, that have set themselves against me round about. ^c3v6

[Psalm 3:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Arise, O LORD; save me, O my God: for thou hast smitten all mine enemies upon the cheek bone; thou hast broken the teeth of the ungodly. ^c3v7

[Psalm 3:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/3?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Salvation belongeth unto the LORD: thy blessing is upon thy people.  Selah. ^c3v8

[Psalm 4:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) HEAR me when I call, O God of my righteousness: thou hast enlarged me when I was in distress; have mercy upon me, and hear my prayer. ^c4v1

[Psalm 4:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) O ye sons of men, how long will ye turn my glory into shame?  how long will ye love vanity, and seek after leasing?  Selah. ^c4v2

[Psalm 4:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) But know that the LORD hath set apart him that is godly for himself: the LORD will hear when I call unto him. ^c4v3

[Psalm 4:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Stand in awe, and sin not: commune with your own heart upon your bed, and be still.  Selah. ^c4v4

[Psalm 4:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Offer the sacrifices of righteousness, and put your trust in the LORD. ^c4v5

[Psalm 4:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) There be many that say, Who will shew us any good?  LORD, lift thou up the light of thy countenance upon us. ^c4v6

[Psalm 4:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Thou hast put gladness in my heart, more than in the time that their corn and their wine increased. ^c4v7

[Psalm 4:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/4?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) I will both lay me down in peace, and sleep: for thou, LORD, only makest me dwell in safety. ^c4v8

[Psalm 5:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) GIVE ear to my words, O LORD, consider my meditation. ^c5v1

[Psalm 5:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Hearken unto the voice of my cry, my King, and my God: for unto thee will I pray. ^c5v2

[Psalm 5:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) My voice shalt thou hear in the morning, O LORD; in the morning will I direct my prayer unto thee, and will look up. ^c5v3

[Psalm 5:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) For thou art not a God that hath pleasure in wickedness: neither shall evil dwell with thee. ^c5v4

[Psalm 5:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) The foolish shall not stand in thy sight: thou hatest all workers of iniquity. ^c5v5

[Psalm 5:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Thou shalt destroy them that speak leasing: the LORD will abhor the bloody and deceitful man. ^c5v6

[Psalm 5:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) But as for me, I will come into thy house in the multitude of thy mercy: and in thy fear will I worship toward thy holy temple. ^c5v7

[Psalm 5:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Lead me, O LORD, in thy righteousness because of mine enemies; make thy way straight before my face. ^c5v8

[Psalm 5:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) For there is no faithfulness in their mouth; their inward part is very wickedness; their throat is an open sepulchre; they flatter with their tongue. ^c5v9

[Psalm 5:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) Destroy thou them, O God; let them fall by their own counsels; cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions; for they have rebelled against thee. ^c5v10

[Psalm 5:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) But let all those that put their trust in thee rejoice: let them ever shout for joy, because thou defendest them: let them also that love thy name be joyful in thee. ^c5v11

[Psalm 5:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/5?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) For thou, LORD, wilt bless the righteous; with favour wilt thou compass him as with a shield. ^c5v12

[Psalm 6:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) O LORD, rebuke me not in thine anger, neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure. ^c6v1

[Psalm 6:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Have mercy upon me, O LORD; for I am weak: O LORD, heal me; for my bones are vexed. ^c6v2

[Psalm 6:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Return, O LORD, deliver my soul: oh save me for thy mercies' sake. ^c6v4

[Psalm 6:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) For in death there is no remembrance of thee: in the grave who shall give thee thanks? ^c6v5

[Psalm 6:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) I am weary with my groaning; all the night make I my bed to swim; I water my couch with my tears. ^c6v6

[Psalm 6:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Mine eye is consumed because of grief; it waxeth old because of all mine enemies. ^c6v7

[Psalm 6:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; for the LORD hath heard the voice of my weeping. ^c6v8

[Psalm 6:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) The LORD hath heard my supplication; the LORD will receive my prayer. ^c6v9

[Psalm 6:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/6?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) Let all mine enemies be ashamed and sore vexed: let them return and be ashamed suddenly. ^c6v10

[Psalm 7:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) O LORD my God, in thee do I put my trust: save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me: ^c7v1

[Psalm 7:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Lest he tear my soul like a lion, rending it in pieces, while there is none to deliver. ^c7v2

[Psalm 7:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) O LORD my God, if I have done this; if there be iniquity in my hands; ^c7v3

[Psalm 7:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) If I have rewarded evil unto him that was at peace with me; (yea, I have delivered him that without cause is mine enemy:) ^c7v4

[Psalm 7:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Let the enemy persecute my soul, and take it; yea, let him tread down my life upon the earth, and lay mine honour in the dust.  Selah. ^c7v5

[Psalm 7:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Arise, O LORD, in thine anger, lift up thyself because of the rage of mine enemies: and awake for me to the judgment that thou hast commanded. ^c7v6

[Psalm 7:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) So shall the congregation of the people compass thee about: for their sakes therefore return thou on high. ^c7v7

[Psalm 7:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) The LORD shall judge the people: judge me, O LORD, according to my righteousness, and according to mine integrity that is in me. ^c7v8

[Psalm 7:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end; but establish the just: for the righteous God trieth the hearts and reins. ^c7v9

[Psalm 7:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) My defence is of God, which saveth the upright in heart. ^c7v10

[Psalm 7:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) God judgeth the righteous, and God is angry with the wicked every day. ^c7v11

[Psalm 7:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) If he turn not, he will whet his sword; he hath bent his bow, and made it ready. ^c7v12

[Psalm 7:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) He hath also prepared for him the instruments of death; he ordaineth his arrows against the persecutors. ^c7v13

[Psalm 7:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, and hath conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood. ^c7v14

[Psalm 7:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) He made a pit, and digged it, and is fallen into the ditch which he made. ^c7v15

[Psalm 7:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) His mischief shall return upon his own head, and his violent dealing shall come down upon his own pate. ^c7v16

[Psalm 7:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/7?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) I will praise the LORD according to his righteousness: and will sing praise to the name of the LORD most high. ^c7v17

[Psalm 8:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) O LORD our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth!  who hast set thy glory above the heavens. ^c8v1

[Psalm 8:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou ordained strength because of thine enemies, that thou mightest still the enemy and the avenger. ^c8v2

[Psalm 8:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) When I consider thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, the moon and the stars, which thou hast ordained; ^c8v3

[Psalm 8:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) What is man, that thou art mindful of him?  and the son of man, that thou visitest him? ^c8v4

[Psalm 8:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) For thou hast made him a little lower than the angels, and hast crowned him with glory and honour. ^c8v5

[Psalm 8:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Thou madest him to have dominion over the works of thy hands; thou hast put all things under his feet: ^c8v6

[Psalm 8:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/8?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) The fowl of the air, and the fish of the sea, and whatsoever passeth through the paths of the seas. ^c8v8

[Psalm 9:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) I WILL praise thee, O LORD, with my whole heart; I will shew forth all thy marvellous works. ^c9v1

[Psalm 9:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will sing praise to thy name, O thou most High. ^c9v2

[Psalm 9:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) When mine enemies are turned back, they shall fall and perish at thy presence. ^c9v3

[Psalm 9:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) For thou hast maintained my right and my cause; thou satest in the throne judging right. ^c9v4

[Psalm 9:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Thou hast rebuked the heathen, thou hast destroyed the wicked, thou hast put out their name for ever and ever. ^c9v5

[Psalm 9:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) O thou enemy, destructions are come to a perpetual end: and thou hast destroyed cities; their memorial is perished with them. ^c9v6

[Psalm 9:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) But the LORD shall endure for ever: he hath prepared his throne for judgment. ^c9v7

[Psalm 9:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And he shall judge the world in righteousness, he shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness. ^c9v8

[Psalm 9:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) The LORD also will be a refuge for the oppressed, a refuge in times of trouble. ^c9v9

[Psalm 9:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And they that know thy name will put their trust in thee: for thou, LORD, hast not forsaken them that seek thee. ^c9v10

[Psalm 9:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Sing praises to the LORD, which dwelleth in Zion: declare among the people his doings. ^c9v11

[Psalm 9:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) When he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth them: he forgetteth not the cry of the humble. ^c9v12

[Psalm 9:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) Have mercy upon me, O LORD; consider my trouble which I suffer of them that hate me, thou that liftest me up from the gates of death: ^c9v13

[Psalm 9:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) That I may shew forth all thy praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion: I will rejoice in thy salvation. ^c9v14

[Psalm 9:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) The heathen are sunk down in the pit that they made: in the net which they hid is their own foot taken. ^c9v15

[Psalm 9:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) The LORD is known by the judgment which he executeth: the wicked is snared in the work of his own hands.  Higgaion.  Selah. ^c9v16

[Psalm 9:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) The wicked shall be turned into hell, and all the nations that forget God. ^c9v17

[Psalm 9:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) For the needy shall not alway be forgotten: the expectation of the poor shall not perish for ever. ^c9v18

[Psalm 9:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) Arise, O LORD; let not man prevail: let the heathen be judged in thy sight. ^c9v19

[Psalm 9:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/9?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) Put them in fear, O LORD: that the nations may know themselves to be but men.  Selah. ^c9v20

[Psalm 10:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) WHY standest thou afar off, O LORD?  why hidest thou thyself in times of trouble? ^c10v1

[Psalm 10:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) The wicked in his pride doth persecute the poor: let them be taken in the devices that they have imagined. ^c10v2

[Psalm 10:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) For the wicked boasteth of his heart's desire, and blesseth the covetous, whom the LORD abhorreth. ^c10v3

[Psalm 10:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, will not seek after God: God is not in all his thoughts. ^c10v4

[Psalm 10:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) His ways are always grievous; thy judgments are far above out of his sight: as for all his enemies, he puffeth at them. ^c10v5

[Psalm 10:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) He hath said in his heart, I shall not be moved: for I shall never be in adversity. ^c10v6

[Psalm 10:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud: under his tongue is mischief and vanity. ^c10v7

[Psalm 10:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) He sitteth in the lurking places of the villages: in the secret places doth he murder the innocent: his eyes are privily set against the poor. ^c10v8

[Psalm 10:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) He lieth in wait secretly as a lion in his den: he lieth in wait to catch the poor: he doth catch the poor, when he draweth him into his net. ^c10v9

[Psalm 10:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) He croucheth, and humbleth himself, that the poor may fall by his strong ones. ^c10v10

[Psalm 10:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) He hath said in his heart, God hath forgotten: he hideth his face; he will never see it. ^c10v11

[Psalm 10:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/10?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Arise, O LORD; O God, lift up thine hand: forget not the humble. ^c10v12

[Psalm 34:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) The angel of the LORD encampeth round about them that fear him, and delivereth them. ^c34v7

[Psalm 34:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) O taste and see that the LORD is good: blessed is the man that trusteth in him. ^c34v8

[Psalm 34:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) O fear the LORD, ye his saints: for there is no want to them that fear him. ^c34v9

[Psalm 34:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger: but they that seek the LORD shall not want any good thing. ^c34v10

[Psalm 34:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Come, ye children, hearken unto me: I will teach you the fear of the LORD. ^c34v11

[Psalm 34:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) What man is he that desireth life, and loveth many days, that he may see good? ^c34v12

[Psalm 34:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) Keep thy tongue from evil, and thy lips from speaking guile. ^c34v13

[Psalm 34:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) Depart from evil, and do good; seek peace, and pursue it. ^c34v14

[Psalm 34:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) The eyes of the LORD are upon the righteous, and his ears are open unto their cry. ^c34v15

[Psalm 34:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) The face of the LORD is against them that do evil, to cut off the remembrance of them from the earth. ^c34v16

[Psalm 34:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) The righteous cry, and the LORD heareth, and delivereth them out of all their troubles. ^c34v17

[Psalm 34:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) The LORD is nigh unto them that are of a broken heart; and saveth such as be of a contrite spirit. ^c34v18

[Psalm 34:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) Many are the afflictions of the righteous: but the LORD delivereth him out of them all. ^c34v19

[Psalm 34:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) He keepeth all his bones: not one of them is broken. ^c34v20

[Psalm 34:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) Evil shall slay the wicked: and they that hate the righteous shall be desolate. ^c34v21

[Psalm 34:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/34?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) The LORD redeemeth the soul of his servants: and none of them that trust in him shall be desolate. ^c34v22

[Psalm 35:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) PLEAD my cause, O LORD, with them that strive with me: fight against them that fight against me. ^c35v1

[Psalm 35:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Take hold of shield and buckler, and stand up for mine help. ^c35v2

[Psalm 35:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Draw out also the spear, and stop the way against them that persecute me: say unto my soul, I am thy salvation. ^c35v3

[Psalm 35:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Let them be confounded and put to shame that seek after my soul: let them be turned back and brought to confusion that devise my hurt. ^c35v4

[Psalm 35:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Let them be as chaff before the wind: and let the angel of the LORD chase them. ^c35v5

[Psalm 35:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Let their way be dark and slippery: and let the angel of the LORD persecute them. ^c35v6

[Psalm 35:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) For without cause have they hid for me their net in a pit, which without cause they have digged for my soul. ^c35v7

[Psalm 35:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Let destruction come upon him at unawares; and let his net that he hath hid catch himself: into that very destruction let him fall. ^c35v8

[Psalm 35:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And my soul shall be joyful in the LORD: it shall rejoice in his salvation. ^c35v9

[Psalm 35:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) All my bones shall say, LORD, who is like unto thee, which deliverest the poor from him that is too strong for him, yea, the poor and the needy from him that spoileth him? ^c35v10

[Psalm 35:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) False witnesses did rise up; they laid to my charge things that I knew not. ^c35v11

[Psalm 35:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) They rewarded me evil for good to the spoiling of my soul. ^c35v12

[Psalm 35:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was sackcloth: I humbled my soul with fasting; and my prayer returned into mine own bosom. ^c35v13

[Psalm 35:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) I behaved myself as though he had been my friend or brother: I bowed down heavily, as one that mourneth for his mother. ^c35v14

[Psalm 35:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) But in mine adversity they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together: yea, the abjects gathered themselves together against me, and I knew it not; they did tear me, and ceased not: ^c35v15

[Psalm 35:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) With hypocritical mockers in feasts, they gnashed upon me with their teeth. ^c35v16

[Psalm 35:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) Lord, how long wilt thou look on?  rescue my soul from their destructions, my darling from the lions. ^c35v17

[Psalm 35:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) I will give thee thanks in the great congregation: I will praise thee among much people. ^c35v18

[Psalm 35:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) Let not them that are mine enemies wrongfully rejoice over me: neither let them wink with the eye that hate me without a cause. ^c35v19

[Psalm 35:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) For they speak not peace: but they devise deceitful matters against them that are quiet in the land. ^c35v20

[Psalm 35:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) Yea, they opened their mouth wide against me, and said, Aha, aha, our eye hath seen it. ^c35v21

[Psalm 35:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) This thou hast seen, O LORD: keep not silence: O Lord, be not far from me. ^c35v22

[Psalm 35:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) Stir up thyself, and awake to my judgment, even unto my cause, my God and my Lord. ^c35v23

[Psalm 35:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) Judge me, O LORD my God, according to thy righteousness; and let them not rejoice over me. ^c35v24

[Psalm 35:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) Let them not say in their hearts, Ah, so would we have it: let them not say, We have swallowed him up. ^c35v25

[Psalm 35:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that rejoice at mine hurt: let them be clothed with shame and dishonour that magnify themselves against me. ^c35v26

[Psalm 35:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) Let them shout for joy, and be glad, that favour my righteous cause: yea, let them say continually, Let the LORD be magnified, which hath pleasure in the prosperity of his servant. ^c35v27

[Psalm 35:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/35?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And my tongue shall speak of thy righteousness and of thy praise all the day long. ^c35v28

[Psalm 36:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) THE transgression of the wicked saith within my heart, that there is no fear of God before his eyes. ^c36v1

[Psalm 36:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit: he hath left off to be wise, and to do good. ^c36v3

[Psalm 36:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) He deviseth mischief upon his bed; he setteth himself in a way that is not good; he abhorreth not evil. ^c36v4

[Psalm 36:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Thy righteousness is like the great mountains; thy judgments are a great deep: O LORD, thou preservest man and beast. ^c36v6

[Psalm 36:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) How excellent is thy lovingkindness, O God!  therefore the children of men put their trust under the shadow of thy wings. ^c36v7

[Psalm 36:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of thy house; and thou shalt make them drink of the river of thy pleasures. ^c36v8

[Psalm 36:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) For with thee is the fountain of life: in thy light shall we see light. ^c36v9

[Psalm 36:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/36?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Let not the foot of pride come against me, and let not the hand of the wicked remove me. ^c36v11

[Psalm 38:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) There is no soundness in my flesh because of thine anger; neither is there any rest in my bones because of my sin. ^c38v3

[Psalm 38:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) For mine iniquities are gone over mine head: as an heavy burden they are too heavy for me. ^c38v4

[Psalm 38:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) My wounds stink and are corrupt because of my foolishness. ^c38v5

[Psalm 38:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) I am troubled; I am bowed down greatly; I go mourning all the day long. ^c38v6

[Psalm 38:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) For my loins are filled with a loathsome disease: and there is no soundness in my flesh. ^c38v7

[Psalm 38:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) I am feeble and sore broken: I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart. ^c38v8

[Psalm 38:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) Lord, all my desire is before thee; and my groaning is not hid from thee. ^c38v9

[Psalm 38:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) My heart panteth, my strength faileth me: as for the light of mine eyes, it also is gone from me. ^c38v10

[Psalm 38:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my sore; and my kinsmen stand afar off. ^c38v11

[Psalm 38:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) They also that seek after my life lay snares for me: and they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and imagine deceits all the day long. ^c38v12

[Psalm 38:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) But I, as a deaf man, heard not; and I was as a dumb man that openeth not his mouth. ^c38v13

[Psalm 38:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) Thus I was as a man that heareth not, and in whose mouth are no reproofs. ^c38v14

[Psalm 38:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) For in thee, O LORD, do I hope: thou wilt hear, O Lord my God. ^c38v15

[Psalm 38:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/38?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) For I said, Hear me, lest otherwise they should rejoice over me: when my foot slippeth, they magnify themselves against me. ^c38v16

[Psalm 64:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/64?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) They encourage themselves in an evil matter: they commune of laying snares privily; they say, Who shall see them? ^c64v5

[Psalm 64:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/64?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) They search out iniquities; they accomplish a diligent search: both the inward thought of every one of them, and the heart, is deep. ^c64v6

[Psalm 64:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/64?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And all men shall fear, and shall declare the work of God; for they shall wisely consider of his doing. ^c64v9

[Psalm 69:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/69?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) They that sit in the gate speak against me; and I was the song of the drunkards. ^c69v12

[Psalm 69:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/69?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) Thou hast known my reproach, and my shame, and my dishonour: mine adversaries are all before thee. ^c69v19

[Psalm 69:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/69?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) Reproach hath broken my heart; and I am full of heaviness: and I looked for some to take pity, but there was none; and for comforters, but I found none. ^c69v20

[Psalm 69:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/69?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) They gave me also gall for my meat; and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink. ^c69v21

[Psalm 75:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/75?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) But God is the judge: he putteth down one, and setteth up another. ^c75v7

[Psalm 75:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/75?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) For in the hand of the LORD there is a cup, and the wine is red; it is full of mixture; and he poureth out of the same: but the dregs thereof, all the wicked of the earth shall wring them out, and drink them. ^c75v8

[Psalm 78:37](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p37#p37) For their heart was not right with him, neither were they stedfast in his covenant. ^c78v37

[Psalm 78:38](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p38#p38) But he, being full of compassion, forgave their iniquity, and destroyed them not: yea, many a time turned he his anger away, and did not stir up all his wrath. ^c78v38

[Psalm 78:39](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p39#p39) For he remembered that they were but flesh; a wind that passeth away, and cometh not again. ^c78v39

[Psalm 78:44](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p44#p44) And had turned their rivers into blood; and their floods, that they could not drink. ^c78v44

[Psalm 78:46](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p46#p46) He gave also their increase unto the caterpiller, and their labour unto the locust. ^c78v46

[Psalm 78:47](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p47#p47) He destroyed their vines with hail, and their sycomore trees with frost. ^c78v47

[Psalm 78:48](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p48#p48) He gave up their cattle also to the hail, and their flocks to hot thunderbolts. ^c78v48

[Psalm 78:49](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p49#p49) He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and indignation, and trouble, by sending evil angels among them. ^c78v49

[Psalm 78:50](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p50#p50) He made a way to his anger; he spared not their soul from death, but gave their life over to the pestilence; ^c78v50

[Psalm 78:51](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p51#p51) And smote all the firstborn in Egypt; the chief of their strength in the tabernacles of Ham: ^c78v51

[Psalm 78:53](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p53#p53) And he led them on safely, so that they feared not: but the sea overwhelmed their enemies. ^c78v53

[Psalm 78:54](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p54#p54) And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, even to this mountain, which his right hand had purchased. ^c78v54

[Psalm 78:58](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p58#p58) For they provoked him to anger with their high places, and moved him to jealousy with their graven images. ^c78v58

[Psalm 78:59](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p59#p59) When God heard this, he was wroth, and greatly abhorred Israel: ^c78v59

[Psalm 78:60](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p60#p60) So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent which he placed among men; ^c78v60

[Psalm 78:61](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p61#p61) And delivered his strength into captivity, and his glory into the enemy's hand. ^c78v61

[Psalm 78:62](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p62#p62) He gave his people over also unto the sword; and was wroth with his inheritance. ^c78v62

[Psalm 78:63](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p63#p63) The fire consumed their young men; and their maidens were not given to marriage. ^c78v63

[Psalm 78:64](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p64#p64) Their priests fell by the sword; and their widows made no lamentation. ^c78v64

[Psalm 78:65](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p65#p65) Then the Lord awaked as one out of sleep, and like a mighty man that shouteth by reason of wine. ^c78v65

[Psalm 78:66](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p66#p66) And he smote his enemies in the hinder parts: he put them to a perpetual reproach. ^c78v66

[Psalm 78:67](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p67#p67) Moreover he refused the tabernacle of Joseph, and chose not the tribe of Ephraim: ^c78v67

[Psalm 78:68](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p68#p68) But chose the tribe of Judah, the mount Zion which he loved. ^c78v68

[Psalm 78:69](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p69#p69) And he built his sanctuary like high palaces, like the earth which he hath established for ever. ^c78v69

[Psalm 78:70](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p70#p70) He chose David also his servant, and took him from the sheepfolds: ^c78v70

[Psalm 78:71](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p71#p71) From following the ewes great with young he brought him to feed Jacob his people, and Israel his inheritance. ^c78v71

[Psalm 78:72](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/78?lang=eng&id=p72#p72) So he fed them according to the integrity of his heart; and guided them by the skilfulness of his hands. ^c78v72

[Psalm 79:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/79?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) O GOD, the heathen are come into thine inheritance; thy holy temple have they defiled; they have laid Jerusalem on heaps. ^c79v1

[Psalm 79:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/79?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) The dead bodies of thy servants have they given to be meat unto the fowls of the heaven, the flesh of thy saints unto the beasts of the earth. ^c79v2

[Psalm 79:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/79?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Their blood have they shed like water round about Jerusalem; and there was none to bury them. ^c79v3

[Psalm 79:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/79?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) We are become a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and derision to them that are round about us. ^c79v4

[Psalm 79:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/79?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) How long, LORD?  wilt thou be angry for ever?  shall thy jealousy burn like fire? ^c79v5

[Psalm 148:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass. ^c148v6

[Psalm 148:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Praise the LORD from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps: ^c148v7

[Psalm 148:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Fire, and hail; snow, and vapour; stormy wind fulfilling his word: ^c148v8

[Psalm 148:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars: ^c148v9

[Psalm 148:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl: ^c148v10

[Psalm 148:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth: ^c148v11

[Psalm 148:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children: ^c148v12

[Psalm 148:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) Let them praise the name of the LORD: for his name alone is excellent; his glory is above the earth and heaven. ^c148v13

[Psalm 148:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/148?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; even of the children of Israel, a people near unto him.  Praise ye the LORD. ^c148v14

[Psalm 149:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) PRAISE ye the LORD.  Sing unto the LORD a new song, and his praise in the congregation of saints. ^c149v1

[Psalm 149:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King. ^c149v2

[Psalm 149:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp. ^c149v3

[Psalm 149:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation. ^c149v4

[Psalm 149:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon their beds. ^c149v5

[Psalm 149:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Let the high praises of God be in their mouth, and a twoedged sword in their hand; ^c149v6

[Psalm 149:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) To execute vengeance upon the heathen, and punishments upon the people; ^c149v7

[Psalm 149:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron; ^c149v8

[Psalm 149:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/149?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) To execute upon them the judgment written: this honour have all his saints.  Praise ye the LORD. ^c149v9

[Psalm 150:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/150?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) PRAISE ye the LORD.  Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power. ^c150v1

[Psalm 150:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/150?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness. ^c150v2

[Psalm 150:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/150?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp. ^c150v3

[Psalm 150:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/150?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs. ^c150v4

[Psalm 150:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/150?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals. ^c150v5

[Psalm 150:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ps/150?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Let every thing that hath breath praise the LORD.  Praise ye the LORD. ^c150v6
